I am a relatively new diver and have only dived in the ocean once before this experience. My first ocean dive was 1.5 years earlier at Catalina Island, and it was a great experience.

Despite the 1.5 year lapse in diving and lack of experience, Laura made me feel super comfortable! We had absolutely terrible visibility the day that we dived which could have been a frightening experience or simply a disappointing one.

Fortunately, Laura informed us of her plan and made adjustments as needed to keep us safe and to make sure that we were able to see as much as possible despite the murky water.

In the ‚ÄúCove‚Äù dive, we were able to swim with playful sea lion pups, and in the ‚ÄúCanyon‚Äù dive, we saw a guitar fish and lots of sand dabs. I highly recommend La Jolla Dive to anyone trying to find a fun, low key, easy to schedule experience renting and diving in the San Diego area. Top notch! I'll definitely be back.< /Text>

<review>We made plans to dive with LJD while visiting from out of town. Scheduling was easy online and while the price was higher than we are used to, especially for a shore dive, we decided to go anyway. We arrived on the dive morning and were fitted with gear which was in great condition and all well taken care of. However, it took 2 hours from when we arrived for us to make our way down to the water for our dives. We were a group of 4, 2 couples, and one couple was more beginner than the other. Unfortunately, despite there being 2 divemasters with us, when one couple was out of air, we were all required to return to shore even though 2 of us had nearly 2000psi left (started with 3000psi). Also, be aware that when you sign up for a 2-tank dive, you will be there all day and they require multiple hours of surface interval between dives and encourage you to go somewhere for lunch. Since it was just our group diving we asked to head into the water for our second dive after just 1 hour of SI but were denied and a lot of frustrations and poor communication ensued which unfortunately soured the whole day for us. Overall, way too much money was spent for services that we did not receive. Maybe if you are a very beginner diver you will enjoy your time here with LJP but for anyone who is used to planning their own dives and has some experience, beware because you will be disappointed.

1572929537734<//time>
<Rating>3<//Rating>< Review>
We stayed at the Spencer Modern. We were a family of four (my husband, myself, and two young children).

Pros:
Check-in was very smooth. Eric the Property Manager greeted us and showed us around. He was very helpful. The home had a surface reno and was clean and very nicely decorated. Very modern. It was perfect for our family. The pool and yard was clean. We went in October and we didn't need the pool heated. I suggest you test the pool out and decide if the temperature is right for you because there is a charge to heating the pool (which is standard throughout Palm Springs). The overall experience was great up until the day we left.

Con:
We booked our stay through Airbnb and we pride ourselves in respecting people's properties as we are landlords ourselves. ONE WEEK later, after we checked-out, an associate from the rental company sent us a bill for $127 for a damaged screen door. Upon our arrival to the unit, there was normal wear and tear throughout the whole house. It was renovated and nice but it wasn't brand new. The patio screen door was already loose and did not shut all the way (I remember this because I was concerned that insects would come in since we have young children). As a result, we avoided using the screen altogether and used the sliding glass door instead. Also we wanted to keep the inside cool. I was appalled to receive the bill. I felt extremely offended since my family use vacation rentals often and we respect people's belongings and properties and never had an issue.

Please be aware of the home itself and take pictures throughout so you are prepared. If you notice wear and tear or ANY sort of small or big damage to the home. Record it. In the off chance that they pin the damage on you, you'll have evidence.

My husband and I are landlords, renovators, and developers ourselves. We know what normal wear and tear is and we know when someone deliberately damage your property. This was not that. We are responsible renters. So to say I'm upset is a great understatement.

I hope this does not happen to you. Otherwise, enjoy your stay. We are fair people and felt like the service during the stay was good, hence the three stars.

< Text>
Found the perfect spot to avoid the poolside and tableside crowds flocking to Palm Springs near festival season. The Casa Tiempo house is perfectly appointed to give your trip a "moved in" feeling. The star of the property is the fantastic backyard pool, lawn, and patio. It's plenty large and plenty private to just sit and soak up the sun. Make a run to the grocery store or have your boxed dinners forwarded to this home because cooking a fantastic meal is a breeze. Nearly every dish, pan, or appliance is here and will save you hours of searching for reservations at one of the limited, tasteful dining options in town.

Tons of bedrooms and the floorplan of the home favors the big glass doors facing the giant backyard. The home is very clean and seems to be well maintained. You have 1 parking space on the property and it's a bit of a chore to get groceries from parking to the kitchen as the garage and back entrance are restricted.

If your top criteria for a home selection is the pool area. This is a top choice. Spa and pool are clean and well maintained. Tons of sunlight exposure and the landscaping is well planned for privacy and visual appeal. Two outdoor fire pits make for some cozy evening gaming. Very happy with the outdoor space.

Couple notes:

1)Assume your coming and going is being monitored. The doors all have sensors and the property owner watches for doors opening that are not locked.
2) Even though the property management book describes how to operate the pool, don't touch or even look at the panel on the wall. The operation demonstrated in the book is incorrect and you will hear from the property manager if you try to get the pool running. Just assume it's running and leave it alone.
3) Ask ALL rental managers if there is construction at any nearby homes. It should be a requirement to disclose any nearby construction, but assume SOMEONE around you is remodeling. Power saws and swimming pools have a way of finding one another.< /Text>

< Review>
99cent coupon at San Diego stores.
Coupon wording is, one free item up to $99.99, free with purchases over $15.00 or more.
But in fact this is not how it works. Items are tallied at register then one lowest price item of a dollar is deducted. Receipt will print wording one item free - $1.00.
Their intent is to get you to come in purchase your fifteen dollars. So if you purchased four things at $5.00 each thinking your going to get one of them for free. Not going to happen! Your only going to get $1.00 off. I guess they can get away with it, because they use the word one free item. This is one way to use manipulation and twisting words to their advantage not the customers. So sad!!<//Review>

< review>
Okay so how many of you are embarrassed to admit that you love shopping at the 99 cent store? Well I'm not! I'm definitely a 99er.

I discovered this particular store when I used to live in the neighborhood many years ago and I've been coming back ever since.

Lots of changes over the years, not least of which is the fact that it's technically not 99 Cents Only anymore since they have more expensive things on the shelves now. Still, they have some incredible bargains on things that you would pay three or four times the amount at Ralph's or Vons or any of the other Supermarket chains.

Nothing luxurious here, but you will definitely save money on staple items and produce. Just be diligent about the condition of things and expiration dates. After all, there's a reason it's at the 99 cent store! The staff are friendly, and they do their best to keep a tidy store. Definitely two thumbs up.</review>

<Text>An incredible place for experienced and beginner reptile keepers alike. Their wide selection of snakes, frogs, lizards, invertebrates, and feeder animals never ceases to impress. The animals are in top notch health, and every employee I've spoken to -at both the Long Beach and Garden Grove locations- have been kind, helpful, and very knowledgeable. I wandered into the Long Beach location after hearing from a coworker that they have cheap bedding/ food that I needed for my new leopard gecko. When I walked in, I was simply amazed. It's rare to find such a small shop with everything as well put together as it is in Reptile Factory. Their invertebrates too! All so well taken care of. Many shops tend to neglect their inverts since they're not as "emotive" or "well loved" as other more popular animals, but not Reptile Factory. Beautiful tarantulas, vinegaroons, and other crawlies were active, happy, and comfortable being handled. The prices were fair for what was available too, I'd be happy to spend more for a new animal knowing it was hand raised coming from such an amazing place. After visiting in Long Beach, I had to see their other location, and drove to Garden Grove the same night. Both shops were exemplary. Please consider giving your business to such compassionate animal keepers. They really deserve all the attention they can get.</Text>< pictures>

< review>
Embarrassed that I didn't realize in time, but they overcharged pretty significantly. Price gouging. From what I can tell, project manager Vicente Oropeza was the driving force on ripping us off. He's more than happy to take advantage of you when you need help most.

Had a pex fitting burst inside a wall inside the house that led to a pretty significant water leak. The on-site plumber Joseph De La Cruz went into the attic and replaced the pex fitting. He said house water pressure was too high (causing the burst) and replaced the pressure reducing valve outside on the water line into the house. He also convinced to put an in-line pressure regulator on there so I can monitor (regrettable in hindsight as it's not necessary, plus pressure valve display was installed upside down).

It's a bit too soon to comment on the quality of the work (other than the upside down pressure valve display) but I can pretty confidently say I was taken for a ride on pricing. Parts were marked up 400%. Plumber told me the pressure reducing valve cost $500 when in reality it's about $125. I looked up the exact part number that was installed so save the 'we buy higher quality stuff' BS.

All in all, they charged me ~$3400 for this. No restoration involved (that part of the company seems more forthright, but they are working with insurance for their $$ so I can't comment on pricing). Just the work described above. That's a good 2 times what a fair price for the work would have been.

In conclusion, I made mistakes allowing this to happen. I was feeling pressure to get the water turned back on for my wife and 2 yo daughter, but at the end of the day, I let this price gouging happen with my poor decision making. At the same time, they were more than glad to rip me off in a time of need and as such, I don't have many nice things to say about the roto-rooter plumbing division and would very much recommend you take your business elsewhere.< /review>
